4397	# Name:          Adobe Glyph List For New Fonts
4398	# Table version: 1.7
4399	# Date:          November 6, 2008
4400	# URL:           https://github.com/adobe-type-tools/agl-aglfn
4401	#
4402	# Description:
4403	#
4404	# AGLFN (Adobe Glyph List For New Fonts) provides a list of base glyph
4405	# names that are recommended for new fonts, which are compatible with
4406	# the AGL (Adobe Glyph List) Specification, and which should be used
4407	# as described in Section 6 of that document. AGLFN comprises the set
4408	# of glyph names from AGL that map via the AGL Specification rules to
4409	# the semantically correct UV (Unicode Value). For example, "Asmall"
4410	# is omitted because AGL maps this glyph name to the PUA (Private Use
4411	# Area) value U+F761, rather than to the UV that maps from the glyph
4412	# name "A." Also omitted is "ffi," because AGL maps this to the
4413	# Alphabetic Presentation Forms value U+FB03, rather than decomposing
4414	# it into the following sequence of three UVs: U+0066, U+0066, and
4415	# U+0069. The name "arrowvertex" has been omitted because this glyph
4416	# now has a real UV, and AGL is now incorrect in mapping it to the PUA
4417	# value U+F8E6. If you do not find an appropriate name for your glyph
4418	# in this list, then please refer to Section 6 of the AGL
4419	# Specification.
4420	#
4421	# Format: three semicolon-delimited fields:
4422	#   (1) Standard UV or CUS UV--four uppercase hexadecimal digits
4423	#   (2) Glyph name--upper/lowercase letters and digits
4424	#   (3) Character names: Unicode character names for standard UVs, and
4425	#       descriptive names for CUS UVs--uppercase letters, hyphen, and
4426	#       space
4427	#
4428	# The records are sorted by glyph name in increasing ASCII order,
4429	# entries with the same glyph name are sorted in decreasing priority
4430	# order, the UVs and Unicode character names are provided for
4431	# convenience, lines starting with "#" are comments, and blank lines
4432	# should be ignored.
4433	#
4434	# Revision History:
4435	#
4436	# 1.7 [6 November 2008]
4437	# - Reverted to the original 1.4 and earlier mappings for Delta,
4438	#   Omega, and mu.
4439	# - Removed mappings for "afii" names. These should now be assigned
4440	#   "uni" names.
4441	# - Removed mappings for "commaaccent" names. These should now be
4442	#   assigned "uni" names.
4443	#
4444	# 1.6 [30 January 2006]
4445	# - Completed work intended in 1.5.
4446	#
4447	# 1.5 [23 November 2005]
4448	# - Removed duplicated block at end of file.
4449	# - Changed mappings:
4450	#   2206;Delta;INCREMENT changed to 0394;Delta;GREEK CAPITAL LETTER DELTA
4451	#   2126;Omega;OHM SIGN changed to 03A9;Omega;GREEK CAPITAL LETTER OMEGA
4452	#   03BC;mu;MICRO SIGN changed to 03BC;mu;GREEK SMALL LETTER MU
4453	# - Corrected statement above about why "ffi" is omitted.
4454	#
4455	# 1.4 [24 September 2003]
4456	# - Changed version to 1.4, to avoid confusion with the AGL 1.3.
4457	# - Fixed spelling errors in the header.
4458	# - Fully removed "arrowvertex," as it is mapped only to a PUA Unicode
4459	#   value in some fonts.
4460	#
4461	# 1.1 [17 April 2003]

4463	#
4464	# 1.0 [31 January 2003]
